Ad Exchange Buyer API

Accesses your bidding-account information, submits creatives for validation, finds available direct deals, and retrieves performance reports.
More information: https://google.com
Contact Info: team@openapitools.org
Version: v1.4
BasePath:/adexchangebuyer/v1.4
Creative Commons Attribution 3.0
http://creativecommons.org/licenses/by/3.0/

Access

  1. OAuth AuthorizationUrl:https://accounts.google.com/o/oauth2/authTokenUrl:
  2. OAuth AuthorizationUrl:https://accounts.google.com/o/oauth2/authTokenUrl:https://accounts.google.com/o/oauth2/token

get /creatives
(adexchangebuyer.creatives.list)
Retrieves a list of the authenticated user's active creatives. A creative will be available 30-40 minutes after submission.

Query parameters

alt (optional)
Query Parameter — Data format for the response. default: null
fields (optional)
Query Parameter — Selector specifying which fields to include in a partial response. default: null

Query Parameter — When specified, only creatives for the given account ids are returned. default: null
buyerCreativeId (optional)
Query Parameter — When specified, only creatives for the given buyer creative ids are returned. default: null
dealsStatusFilter (optional)

Query Parameter — A continuation token, used to page through ad clients. To retrieve the next page, set this parameter to the value of "nextPageToken" from the previous response. Optional. default: null

200

Successful response DeleteOrderDealsResponse
Up 
post /proposals/{proposalId}/deals/insert
(adexchangebuyer.marketplacedeals.insert)
Add new deals for the specified proposal

proposalId (required)
Path Parameter — proposalId for which deals need to be added. default: null

  • application/json

Produces

This API call produces the following media types according to the Accept request header; the media type will be conveyed by the Content-Type response header.
  • application/json

Responses

200

Successful response AddOrderDealsResponse
Up 
get /proposals/{proposalId}/deals
(adexchangebuyer.marketplacedeals.list)
List all the deals for a given proposal

Path parameters

proposalId (required)
Path Parameter — The proposalId to get deals for. To search across all proposals specify order_id = '-' as part of the URL. default: null

Query parameters

alt (optional)
Query Parameter — Data format for the response. default: null
fields (optional)
Query Parameter — Selector specifying which fields to include in a partial response. default: null
key (optional)
Query Parameter — API key. Your API key identifies your project and provides you with API access, quota, and reports. Required unless you provide an OAuth 2.0 token. default: null
oauth_token (optional)
Query Parameter — OAuth 2.0 token for the current user. default: null
prettyPrint (optional)
Query Parameter — Returns response with indentations and line breaks. default: null
quotaUser (optional)
Query Parameter — An opaque string that represents a user for quota purposes. Must not exceed 40 characters. default: null
userIp (optional)
Query Parameter — Deprecated. Please use quotaUser instead. default: null
pqlQuery (optional)
Query Parameter — Query string to retrieve specific deals. default: null

Return type

GetOrderDealsResponse

Produces

This API call produces the following media types according to the Accept request header; the media type will be conveyed by the Content-Type response header.

Responses

200

Successful response GetOrderDealsResponse
Up 
post /proposals/{proposalId}/deals/update
(adexchangebuyer.marketplacedeals.update)
Replaces all the deals in the proposal with the passed in deals

proposalId (required)
Path Parameter — The proposalId to edit deals on. default: null

Produces

This API call produces the following media types according to the Accept request header; the media type will be conveyed by the Content-Type response header.
  • application/json

Responses

200

Successful response Product
Up 
get /products/search
(adexchangebuyer.products.search)
Gets the requested product.

Query parameters

alt (optional)
Query Parameter — Data format for the response. default: null
fields (optional)
Query Parameter — Selector specifying which fields to include in a partial response. default: null
key (optional)
Query Parameter — API key. Your API key identifies your project and provides you with API access, quota, and reports. Required unless you provide an OAuth 2.0 token. default: null
oauth_token (optional)
Query Parameter — OAuth 2.0 token for the current user. default: null
prettyPrint (optional)
Query Parameter — Returns response with indentations and line breaks. default: null
quotaUser (optional)
Query Parameter — An opaque string that represents a user for quota purposes. Must not exceed 40 characters. default: null
userIp (optional)
Query Parameter — Deprecated. Please use quotaUser instead. default: null
pqlQuery (optional)
Query Parameter — The pql query used to query for products. default: null

patch /proposals/{proposalId}/{revisionNumber}/{updateAction}
(adexchangebuyer.proposals.patch)
Update the given proposal. This method supports patch semantics.

Path parameters

proposalId (required)
Path Parameter — The proposal id to update. default: null
revisionNumber (required)
Path Parameter — The last known revision number to update. If the head revision in the marketplace database has since changed, an error will be thrown. The caller should then fetch the latest proposal at head revision and retry the update at that revision. default: null
updateAction (required)
Path Parameter — The proposed action to take on the proposal. This field is required and it must be set when updating a proposal. default: null

Account - Up

Configuration data for an Ad Exchange buyer account.
applyPretargetingToNonGuaranteedDeals (optional)
Boolean When this is false, bid requests that include a deal ID for a private auction or preferred deal are always sent to your bidder. When true, all active pretargeting configs will be applied to private auctions and preferred deals. Programmatic Guaranteed deals (when enabled) are always sent to your bidder.
bidderLocation (optional)
array[Account_bidderLocation_inner] Your bidder locations that have distinct URLs.
cookieMatchingNid (optional)
String The nid parameter value used in cookie match requests. Please contact your technical account manager if you need to change this.
cookieMatchingUrl (optional)
String The base URL used in cookie match requests.
id (optional)
Integer Account id. format: int32
kind (optional)
String Resource type.
maximumActiveCreatives (optional)
Integer The maximum number of active creatives that an account can have, where a creative is active if it was inserted or bid with in the last 30 days. Please contact your technical account manager if you need to change this. format: int32
maximumTotalQps (optional)
Integer The sum of all bidderLocation.maximumQps values cannot exceed this. Please contact your technical account manager if you need to change this. format: int32
numberActiveCreatives (optional)
Integer The number of creatives that this account inserted or bid with in the last 30 days. format: int32

Account_bidderLocation_inner - Up

bidProtocol (optional)
String

The protocol that the bidder endpoint is using. OpenRTB protocols with prefix PROTOCOL_OPENRTB_PROTOBUF use proto buffer, otherwise use JSON. Allowed values:

  • PROTOCOL_ADX
  • PROTOCOL_OPENRTB_2_2
  • PROTOCOL_OPENRTB_2_3
  • PROTOCOL_OPENRTB_2_4
  • PROTOCOL_OPENRTB_2_5
  • PROTOCOL_OPENRTB_PROTOBUF_2_3
  • PROTOCOL_OPENRTB_PROTOBUF_2_4
  • PROTOCOL_OPENRTB_PROTOBUF_2_5
maximumQps (optional)
Integer The maximum queries per second the Ad Exchange will send. format: int32
region (optional)
String

The geographical region the Ad Exchange should send requests from. Only used by some quota systems, but always setting the value is recommended. Allowed values:

  • ASIA
  • EUROPE
  • US_EAST
  • US_WEST
url (optional)
String The URL to which the Ad Exchange will send bid requests.

Creative - Up

A creative and its classification data.
HTMLSnippet (optional)
String The HTML snippet that displays the ad when inserted in the web page. If set, videoURL, videoVastXML, and nativeAd should not be set.
accountId (optional)
Integer Account id. format: int32
adChoicesDestinationUrl (optional)
String The link to the Ad Preferences page. This is only supported for native ads.
adTechnologyProviders (optional)
Creative_adTechnologyProviders
advertiserId (optional)
array[String] Detected advertiser id, if any. Read-only. This field should not be set in requests. format: int64
advertiserName (optional)
String The name of the company being advertised in the creative. A list of advertisers is provided in the advertisers.txt file.
agencyId (optional)
String The agency id for this creative. format: int64
apiUploadTimestamp (optional)
Date The last upload timestamp of this creative if it was uploaded via API. Read-only. The value of this field is generated, and will be ignored for uploads. (formatted RFC 3339 timestamp). format: date-time
attribute (optional)
array[Integer] List of buyer selectable attributes for the ads that may be shown from this snippet. Each attribute is represented by an integer as defined in buyer-declarable-creative-attributes.txt. format: int32
buyerCreativeId (optional)
String A buyer-specific id identifying the creative in this ad.
clickThroughUrl (optional)
array[String] The set of destination urls for the snippet.
corrections (optional)
array[Creative_corrections_inner] Shows any corrections that were applied to this creative. Read-only. This field should not be set in requests.
creativeStatusIdentityType (optional)
String Creative status identity type that the creative item applies to. Ad Exchange real-time bidding is migrating to the sizeless creative verification. Originally, Ad Exchange assigned creative verification status to a unique combination of a buyer creative ID and creative dimensions. Post-migration, a single verification status will be assigned at the buyer creative ID level. This field allows to distinguish whether a given creative status applies to a unique combination of a buyer creative ID and creative dimensions, or to a buyer creative ID as a whole.
dealsStatus (optional)
String Top-level deals status. Read-only. This field should not be set in requests. If disapproved, an entry for auctionType=DIRECT_DEALS (or ALL) in servingRestrictions will also exist. Note that this may be nuanced with other contextual restrictions, in which case it may be preferable to read from servingRestrictions directly.
detectedDomains (optional)
array[String] Detected domains for this creative. Read-only. This field should not be set in requests.
filteringReasons (optional)
Creative_filteringReasons
height (optional)
Integer Ad height. format: int32
impressionTrackingUrl (optional)
array[String] The set of urls to be called to record an impression.
kind (optional)
String Resource type.
languages (optional)
array[String] Detected languages for this creative. Read-only. This field should not be set in requests.
nativeAd (optional)
Creative_nativeAd
openAuctionStatus (optional)
String Top-level open auction status. Read-only. This field should not be set in requests. If disapproved, an entry for auctionType=OPEN_AUCTION (or ALL) in servingRestrictions will also exist. Note that this may be nuanced with other contextual restrictions, in which case it may be preferable to read from ServingRestrictions directly.
productCategories (optional)
array[Integer] Detected product categories, if any. Each category is represented by an integer as defined in ad-product-categories.txt. Read-only. This field should not be set in requests. format: int32
restrictedCategories (optional)
array[Integer] All restricted categories for the ads that may be shown from this snippet. Each category is represented by an integer as defined in the ad-restricted-categories.txt. format: int32
sensitiveCategories (optional)
array[Integer] Detected sensitive categories, if any. Each category is represented by an integer as defined in ad-sensitive-categories.txt. Read-only. This field should not be set in requests. format: int32
servingRestrictions (optional)
array[Creative_servingRestrictions_inner] The granular status of this ad in specific contexts. A context here relates to where something ultimately serves (for example, a physical location, a platform, an HTTPS vs HTTP request, or the type of auction). Read-only. This field should not be set in requests. See the examples in the Creatives guide for more details.
vendorType (optional)
array[Integer] List of vendor types for the ads that may be shown from this snippet. Each vendor type is represented by an integer as defined in vendors.txt. format: int32
version (optional)
Integer The version for this creative. Read-only. This field should not be set in requests. format: int32
videoURL (optional)
String The URL to fetch a video ad. If set, HTMLSnippet, videoVastXML, and nativeAd should not be set. Note, this is different from resource.native_ad.video_url above.
videoVastXML (optional)
String The contents of a VAST document for a video ad. This document should conform to the VAST 2.0 or 3.0 standard. If set, HTMLSnippet, videoURL, and nativeAd and should not be set.
width (optional)
Integer Ad width. format: int32

Creative_adTechnologyProviders - Up

detectedProviderIds (optional)
array[String] The detected ad technology provider IDs for this creative. See https://storage.googleapis.com/adx-rtb-dictionaries/providers.csv for mapping of provider ID to provided name, a privacy policy URL, and a list of domains which can be attributed to the provider. If this creative contains provider IDs that are outside of those listed in the BidRequest.adslot.consented_providers_settings.consented_providers field on the Authorized Buyers Real-Time Bidding protocol or the BidRequest.user.ext.consented_providers_settings.consented_providers field on the OpenRTB protocol, a bid submitted for a European Economic Area (EEA) user with this creative is not compliant with the GDPR policies as mentioned in the "Third-party Ad Technology Vendors" section of Authorized Buyers Program Guidelines. format: int64
hasUnidentifiedProvider (optional)
Boolean Whether the creative contains an unidentified ad technology provider. If true, a bid submitted for a European Economic Area (EEA) user with this creative is not compliant with the GDPR policies as mentioned in the "Third-party Ad Technology Vendors" section of Authorized Buyers Program Guidelines.

EditAllOrderDealsRequest - Up

deals (optional)
array[MarketplaceDeal] List of deals to edit. Service may perform 3 different operations based on comparison of deals in this list vs deals already persisted in database: 1. Add new deal to proposal If a deal in this list does not exist in the proposal, the service will create a new deal and add it to the proposal. Validation will follow AddOrderDealsRequest. 2. Update existing deal in the proposal If a deal in this list already exist in the proposal, the service will update that existing deal to this new deal in the request. Validation will follow UpdateOrderDealsRequest. 3. Delete deals from the proposal (just need the id) If a existing deal in the proposal is not present in this list, the service will delete that deal from the proposal. Validation will follow DeleteOrderDealsRequest.
proposal (optional)
Proposal
proposalRevisionNumber (optional)
String The last known revision number for the proposal. format: int64
updateAction (optional)
String Indicates an optional action to take on the proposal

EditAllOrderDealsResponse - Up

deals (optional)
array[MarketplaceDeal] List of all deals in the proposal after edit.
orderRevisionNumber (optional)
String The latest revision number after the update has been applied. format: int64

PretargetingConfig - Up

billingId (optional)
String The id for billing purposes, provided for reference. Leave this field blank for insert requests; the id will be generated automatically. format: int64
configId (optional)
String The config id; generated automatically. Leave this field blank for insert requests. format: int64
configName (optional)
String The name of the config. Must be unique. Required for all requests.
creativeType (optional)
array[String] List must contain exactly one of PRETARGETING_CREATIVE_TYPE_HTML or PRETARGETING_CREATIVE_TYPE_VIDEO.
dimensions (optional)
array[PretargetingConfig_dimensions_inner] Requests which allow one of these (width, height) pairs will match. All pairs must be supported ad dimensions.
excludedContentLabels (optional)
array[String] Requests with any of these content labels will not match. Values are from content-labels.txt in the downloadable files section. format: int64
excludedGeoCriteriaIds (optional)
array[String] Requests containing any of these geo criteria ids will not match. format: int64
excludedPlacements (optional)
array[PretargetingConfig_excludedPlacements_inner] Requests containing any of these placements will not match.
excludedUserLists (optional)
array[String] Requests containing any of these users list ids will not match. format: int64
excludedVerticals (optional)
array[String] Requests containing any of these vertical ids will not match. Values are from the publisher-verticals.txt file in the downloadable files section. format: int64
geoCriteriaIds (optional)
array[String] Requests containing any of these geo criteria ids will match. format: int64
isActive (optional)
Boolean Whether this config is active. Required for all requests.
kind (optional)
String The kind of the resource, i.e. "adexchangebuyer#pretargetingConfig".
languages (optional)
array[String] Request containing any of these language codes will match.
maximumQps (optional)
String The maximum QPS allocated to this pretargeting configuration, used for pretargeting-level QPS limits. By default, this is not set, which indicates that there is no QPS limit at the configuration level (a global or account-level limit may still be imposed). format: int64
minimumViewabilityDecile (optional)
Integer Requests where the predicted viewability is below the specified decile will not match. E.g. if the buyer sets this value to 5, requests from slots where the predicted viewability is below 50% will not match. If the predicted viewability is unknown this field will be ignored. format: int32
mobileCarriers (optional)
array[String] Requests containing any of these mobile carrier ids will match. Values are from mobile-carriers.csv in the downloadable files section. format: int64
mobileDevices (optional)
array[String] Requests containing any of these mobile device ids will match. Values are from mobile-devices.csv in the downloadable files section. format: int64
mobileOperatingSystemVersions (optional)
array[String] Requests containing any of these mobile operating system version ids will match. Values are from mobile-os.csv in the downloadable files section. format: int64
placements (optional)
array[PretargetingConfig_excludedPlacements_inner] Requests containing any of these placements will match.
platforms (optional)
array[String] Requests matching any of these platforms will match. Possible values are PRETARGETING_PLATFORM_MOBILE, PRETARGETING_PLATFORM_DESKTOP, and PRETARGETING_PLATFORM_TABLET.
supportedCreativeAttributes (optional)
array[String] Creative attributes should be declared here if all creatives corresponding to this pretargeting configuration have that creative attribute. Values are from pretargetable-creative-attributes.txt in the downloadable files section. format: int64
userIdentifierDataRequired (optional)
array[String] Requests containing the specified type of user data will match. Possible values are HOSTED_MATCH_DATA, which means the request is cookie-targetable and has a match in the buyer's hosted match table, and COOKIE_OR_IDFA, which means the request has either a targetable cookie or an iOS IDFA.
userLists (optional)
array[String] Requests containing any of these user list ids will match. format: int64
vendorTypes (optional)
array[String] Requests that allow any of these vendor ids will match. Values are from vendors.txt in the downloadable files section. format: int64
verticals (optional)
array[String] Requests containing any of these vertical ids will match. format: int64
videoPlayerSizes (optional)
array[PretargetingConfig_videoPlayerSizes_inner] Video requests satisfying any of these player size constraints will match.

PricePerBuyer - Up

Used to specify pricing rules for buyers. Each PricePerBuyer in a product can become [0,1] deals. To check if there is a PricePerBuyer for a particular buyer we look for the most specific matching rule - we first look for a rule matching the buyer and otherwise look for a matching rule where no buyer is set.
auctionTier (optional)
String Optional access type for this buyer.

Product - Up

A product is segment of inventory that a seller wishes to sell. It is associated with certain terms and targeting information which helps buyer know more about the inventory. Each field in a product can have one of the following setting:

(readonly) - It is an error to try and set this field. (buyer-readonly) - Only the seller can set this field. (seller-readonly) - Only the buyer can set this field. (updatable) - The field is updatable at all times by either buyer or the seller.

billedBuyer (optional)
Buyer
buyer (optional)
Buyer
creationTimeMs (optional)
String Creation time in ms. since epoch (readonly) format: int64
creatorContacts (optional)
array[ContactInformation] Optional contact information for the creator of this product. (buyer-readonly)
creatorRole (optional)
String The role that created the offer. Set to BUYER for buyer initiated offers.
deliveryControl (optional)
DeliveryControl
flightEndTimeMs (optional)
String The proposed end time for the deal (ms since epoch) (buyer-readonly) format: int64
flightStartTimeMs (optional)
String Inventory availability dates. (times are in ms since epoch) The granularity is generally in the order of seconds. (buyer-readonly) format: int64
hasCreatorSignedOff (optional)
Boolean If the creator has already signed off on the product, then the buyer can finalize the deal by accepting the product as is. When copying to a proposal, if any of the terms are changed, then auto_finalize is automatically set to false.
inventorySource (optional)
String What exchange will provide this inventory (readonly, except on create).
kind (optional)
String Identifies what kind of resource this is. Value: the fixed string "adexchangebuyer#product".

name (optional)

privateAuctionId (optional)
String Optional private auction id if this offer is a private auction offer.
productId (optional)

publisherProfileId (optional)
String Id of the publisher profile for a given seller. A (seller.account_id, publisher_profile_id) pair uniquely identifies a publisher profile. Buyers can call the PublisherProfiles::List endpoint to get a list of publisher profiles for a given seller.

Proposal - Up

Represents a proposal in the marketplace. A proposal is the unit of negotiation between a seller and a buyer and contains deals which are served. Each field in a proposal can have one of the following setting:

(readonly) - It is an error to try and set this field. (buyer-readonly) - Only the seller can set this field. (seller-readonly) - Only the buyer can set this field. (updatable) - The field is updatable at all times by either buyer or the seller.

billedBuyer (optional)
Buyer
buyer (optional)
Buyer
buyerContacts (optional)
array[ContactInformation] Optional contact information of the buyer. (seller-readonly)
buyerPrivateData (optional)
PrivateData

array[String] IDs of DBM advertisers permission to this proposal.
hasBuyerSignedOff (optional)
Boolean When an proposal is in an accepted state, indicates whether the buyer has signed off. Once both sides have signed off on a deal, the proposal can be finalized by the seller. (seller-readonly)
hasSellerSignedOff (optional)
Boolean When an proposal is in an accepted state, indicates whether the buyer has signed off Once both sides have signed off on a deal, the proposal can be finalized by the seller. (buyer-readonly)
inventorySource (optional)
String What exchange will provide this inventory (readonly, except on create).
isRenegotiating (optional)
Boolean True if the proposal is being renegotiated (readonly).
isSetupComplete (optional)
Boolean True, if the buyside inventory setup is complete for this proposal. (readonly, except via OrderSetupCompleted action) Deprecated in favor of deal level setup complete flag.
kind (optional)
String Identifies what kind of resource this is. Value: the fixed string "adexchangebuyer#proposal".
labels (optional)
array[MarketplaceLabel] List of labels associated with the proposal. (readonly)
